      781 +                                                              
      782 +export class PromptRollbackManager {                          
      783 +  async rollback(agentType: string, toVersion?: number):      
          +Promise<void> {                                               
      784 +    const history = await this.getHistory(agentType);         
      785 +                                                              
      786 +    if (toVersion) {                                          
      787 +      // å›æ»šåˆ°æŒ‡å®šç‰ˆæœ¬

      790 +    } else {                                                  
      791 +      // å›æ»šåˆ°ä¸Šä¸€ä¸ªç‰ˆæœ¬                                        
          

      792 +      const current = history[0];

      822 +                                                              
      823 +```typescript                                                 
      824 +// src/evolution/failure-queue.ts                             
      825 +                                                              
      826 +export interface FailedOperation {                            
      827 +  id: string;                                                 
      828 +  operation: 'knowledge_write' | 'vector_store' |             
          +'prompt_update';                                              
      829 +  payload: unknown;                                           
      830 +  error: string;                                              
      831 +  timestamp: string;                                          
      832 +  retryCount: number;                                         
      833 +  maxRetries: number;                                         
      834 +  nextRetryAt: string;                                        
      835 +}                                                             
      836 +                                                              
      837 +export class FailureQueue {                                   
      838 +  private queue: FailedOperation[] = [];                      
      839 +                                                              
      840 +  async enqueue(operation: FailedOperation): Promise<void> {  
      841 +    this.queue.push(operation);                               
      842 +    await this.persist();                                     
      843 +  }                                                           
      844 +                                                              
      845 +  async retry(): Promise<void> {                              
      846 +    const now = new Date().toISOString();                     
      847 +    const readyToRetry = this.queue.filter(op =>              
          +op.nextRetryAt <= now);                                       
      848 +                                                              
      849 +    for (const op of readyToRetry) {                          
      850 +      try {                                                   
      851 +        await this.executeOperation(op);                      
      852 +        await this.remove(op.id);                             
      853 +      } catch (error) {                                       
      854 +        op.retryCount++;                                      
      855 +        if (op.retryCount >= op.maxRetries) {                 
      856 +          // è¾¾åˆ°æœ€å¤§é‡è¯•æ¬¡æ•°ï¼Œç§»åˆ°æ­»ä¿¡é˜Ÿåˆ—                      
                 

      857 +          await this.moveToDeadLetter(op);                    
      858 +        } else {                                              
      859 +          // æŒ‡æ•°é€€é¿                                            
      

      860 +          op.nextRetryAt =                                    
          +this.calculateNextRetry(op.retryCount);                       
      861 +        }                                                     
      862 +      }                                                       
      863 +    }                                                         
      864 +  }                                                           
      865 +                                                              
      866 +  private calculateNextRetry(retryCount: number): string {    
      867 +    const delay = Math.min(1000 * Math.pow(2, retryCount),    
          +60000); // æœ€å¤§1åˆ†é’Ÿ                                             
      

      868 +    return new Date(Date.now() + delay).toISOString();        
      869 +  }                                                           
      870 +}                                                             
      871 +```                                                           
      872 +

          +Promise<void> {

      785 +

      822 +                                                              
      823 +```typescript                                                 
      824 +// src/evolution/failure-queue.ts                             
      825 +                                                              
      826 +export interface FailedOperation {                            
      827 +  id: string;                                                 
      828 +  operation: 'knowledge_write' | 'vector_store' |             
          +'prompt_update';                                              
      829 +  payload: unknown;                                           
      830 +  error: string;                                              
      831 +  timestamp: string;                                          
      832 +  retryCount: number;                                         
      833 +  maxRetries: number;                                         
      834 +  nextRetryAt: string;                                        
      835 +}                                                             
      836 +                                                              
      837 +export class FailureQueue {                                   
      838 +  private queue: FailedOperation[] = [];                      
      839 +                                                              
      840 +  async enqueue(operation: FailedOperation): Promise<void> {  
      841 +    this.queue.push(operation);                               
      842 +    await this.persist();                                     
      843 +  }                                                           
      844 +                                                              
      845 +  async retry(): Promise<void> {                              
      846 +    const now = new Date().toISOString();                     
      847 +    const readyToRetry = this.queue.filter(op =>              
          +op.nextRetryAt <= now);                                       
      848 +                                                              
      849 +    for (const op of readyToRetry) {                          
      850 +      try {                                                   
      851 +        await this.executeOperation(op);                      
      852 +        await this.remove(op.id);                             
      853 +      } catch (error) {                                       
      854 +        op.retryCount++;                                      
      855 +        if (op.retryCount >= op.maxRetries) {                 
      856 +          // è¾¾åˆ°æœ€å¤§é‡è¯•æ¬¡æ•°ï¼Œç§»åˆ°æ­»ä¿¡é˜Ÿåˆ—                      
                 

      857 +          await this.moveToDeadLetter(op);                    
      858 +        } else {                                              
      859 +          // æŒ‡æ•°é€€é¿                                            
      

      860 +          op.nextRetryAt =                                    
          +this.calculateNextRetry(op.retryCount);                       
      861 +        }                                                     
      862 +      }                                                       
      863 +    }                                                         
      864 +  }                                                           
      865 +                                                              
      866 +  private calculateNextRetry(retryCount: number): string {    
      867 +    const delay = Math.min(1000 * Math.pow(2, retryCount),    
          +60000); // æœ€å¤§1åˆ†é’Ÿ                                             
      

      868 +    return new Date(Date.now() + delay).toISOString();        
      869 +  }                                                           
      870 +}                                                             
      871 +```                                                           
      872 +
